# sim-lab · outbox

> **Sole writer: this Project. Append-only.** Finalized verdicts in the kit ORDER
> grammar (see README.md § Verdict grammar), addressed to the **fleet manager** — it
> final-reviews every entry at its :30 sweeps and owns all post-verdict routing; this
> lane never dispatches work to other repos. A verdict only lands here after its report
> passed the validity gate AND its PR carries the @codex comment (Q-0264.4). Entries are
> never edited after append — a superseded verdict gets a new entry that names the old
> one.

idea: idea-engine `control/outbox.md` PROPOSAL 004 · 2026-07-10T21:25:30Z, pinned https://github.com/menno420/idea-engine/blob/cd7251ec30950d12d29e65c57d843864387d0aec/control/outbox.md (canonical superbot `docs/ideas/explore-hub-federated-world-2026-06-19.md` @ fd638e3c0693687a62093aa6bd75954e238fa58d)
verdict: needs-more-evidence
evidence: simulation    # rung 1 — 5 seeds, deterministic, byte-identical re-runs, full 300-cell sweep (trickle × effect × mechanism × veteran depth), 4469 self-checks; the load-bearing claim is a construction identity self-checked to exact 0 on every cell
report: sims/verdict-004-explore-hub-xp-balance/ (PR #13, merge 4d84037ba005e22ee2b2f94facea8bb20105bed2) · run: `python3 sims/verdict-004-explore-hub-xp-balance/federated_xp_balance_sim.py`
recommendation: SETTLED (structural, gate-PASS) — the safety of "loops accelerate, never gate" is a MECHANISM property, not a magnitude one: model global skills as RATE/efficiency multipliers only (phi=0 — stamina/xp-gain/movement, never flat in-game power) and substitution is 0 and the global-only content band is 0 at EVERY swept effect size and trickle ratio (mechanism-sweep phi=0 row all zeros, asserted exact). Any power-contributing design (phi>0) makes global level substitute for mastery AND gate content, monotonically in phi·e (worst swept cell phi=1.0,e=0.50 → a game-novice reaches 0.776 of a master's competence and opens a 0.50-wide global-only content gate). Ship the phi=0 mechanism constraint as the INVARIANT; content thresholds must be ≤ pure-per-game max (any unlock requiring global level = contract violation). PROVISIONAL magnitude (a UX dial, pending telemetry): trickle t≈0.10, effect budget e≈0.20–0.35, hard BOOST_CAP≈0.25 — at e=0.20 a moderate veteran's cold-start advantage is 0.091 (just under the 0.10 "measurable" line) while deep veterans clear it (0.167), and e≈0.35 clears it across depths (0.141–0.258). UNSETTLED (hypothesis) — the exact effect magnitude rides on family-level earn-shape stand-ins + an assumed session model, and the secondary rate→faster-leveling→power channel is unmodeled. TELEMETRY PR 2's plumbing slice MUST log to close the gap: per-session earn + source game; session length; global_frac at each new-game start; sessions/time-to-baseline (L_BASE) per new game; per-game-level vs global-level at every content-unlock event (the gate-violation tripwire); trickle inflow rate per game. OUT OF SCOPE (owner-reserved): hub shape, survival overlay, docking topology, cross-game identity.
codex: PR #13 comment https://github.com/menno420/sim-lab/pull/13#issuecomment-4940156540 (one question: does the phi=0 "never substitutes for mastery" guarantee survive the unmodeled secondary channel — a rate-only boost still lets a veteran reach any per-game level faster; is faster-mastery the intended accelerator or a de-facto substitute needing a tighter BOOST_CAP?) · reply: pending (OA-002 open — Codex GitHub integration not yet enabled for sim-lab; fold in when it lands, verify against tree first)
gate: PASS (structural claim — rate-only/phi=0 global skills cannot substitute for mastery or gate content at any swept magnitude — is uncorrupted [4469 self-checks + analytic-tie + byte-identical re-runs], robust [0 by construction at every axis edge], reproducible [one command, stdlib-only, 5 seeds]; the COMPARABLE-TO-LIVE gap touches ONLY the magnitude recommendation, which is carried explicitly as a hypothesis, not evidence — hence verdict needs-more-evidence, not approve)

measured: full pre-registered grid (36 envelope cells = 3 archetypes × 4 edges × 3 caps; 5 swept policies × 3 profiles per cell; M = 5,000 casual / 2,000 grinder / 500 compulsive per cell-policy, seed 20260721, pinned loop order, one rng.random() draw per bet; decisions in exact integer cross-multiplication) — REJECT BINDS: E*(g, m) = ∅ in 36/36 cells, at every cap, in 3/3 archetypes (bar: 2/3), both arms where covered (c_leg_band_side_flips empty — MC and the exact arm agree on every band side Arm A covers), stability-reproduced; ANATOMY: SINK fails 33/36 — for G2 (k=5) and G3 (k=19) NO edge at NO cap passes: worst-policy P_double 0.195–0.323 vs the 0.10 band, because p = (1−e)/(k+1) moves only by the factor (1−e) as e sweeps the grid (k=19: p 0.0495 → 0.045), so the grinder's doubling odds are variance-dominated, not edge-controlled (e=0 control measures 0.30–0.41 on the same cells — a 10% edge buys back a few points, never the 2–3× needed); only even-money G1 is edge-controllable (the closed-form leg): SINK passes exactly at (e=0.05, m=0.05) 0.0895 (Arm A exact for the binding C policy: 0.0899), (e=0.10, m=0.05) 0.0170, (e=0.10, m=0.25) 0.0975; SAFE fails 36/36 — flat C-50 wipes 0.063–0.725 at the tight cap m=0.05, capped martingale wipes 0.182–0.983 at m ≥ 0.25, and even at the e=0 control C-50 wipes 5.7%: wipe-within-100-bets is gambler's-ruin VARIANCE, not edge, so no odds setting can satisfy the band; FUN fails only 3/36 (Arm A exact: G1 e=0.10 at 0.1346 < 0.25; G2 holds 0.4879–0.3275 and G3 0.3750–0.2950 across the whole grid — high-variance shapes stay winnable at every edge, which is exactly why they cannot be sink-proofed); NEAREST MISS quantified: (G1, e=0.05, m=0.05) passes FUN (0.2738 exact) AND SINK (0.0895) but fails SAFE at 2.7× the band (P_wipe 0.1358 via flat C-50; the tight cap tames martingale to 0.007 there); PRE-REGISTERED GAP (FUN at the smallest SINK-passing edge): G1 m=0.05 → e=0.05, FUN 0.2738 (SAFE is the killer, not FUN); G1 m=0.25 → e=0.10, FUN 0.1346 (the classic fun/sink tension); G1 m=1.0 and ALL of G2/G3 at every cap → NO SINK-passing edge in-grid (gap unbounded — the odds lever cannot reach it); INDETERMINACY touched nothing: 7 cells carry > 1% grinder cap-hits (F-0.01's slow walk; max 0.376) but every one fails DEFINITIVELY (FUN analytic, SAFE sessions always complete, measured P_double a lower bound), so the NULL routing was never load-bearing; VALIDITY: agreement gate PASS — pooled per-edge G1×C deviations 0.051–0.720 pp vs the 1.0 pp gate, e=0 control reproduces P_double = 1/3 (closed form == independent tridiagonal elimination, exact, all edges), per-cap deviations disclosed (4/15 exceed 1.0 pp, max 1.93 pp, consistent with the ~1.05 pp per-cap SE the pooling disclosure anticipated); aux reference-leg MC agrees with the exact binomial tails on all 15 cells within 4 SE; stability leg (seed 20260722, half M) reproduces REJECT with the identical all-36-empty envelope; COMPULSIVE harm context (reporting-only): median 40 flat bets to ruin on G3 at ANY edge (m=1.0), 92–173 on G2, 160–525 on G1, ruin fraction ≥ 0.98 at every e ≥ 0.01; recommendation: enforce the pre-registered REJECT consequence — tonight's minigame/casino consolidation does NOT tune per-game odds hoping to reconcile fun with sink-proofing (the sim proves the reconciliation does not exist inside the odds lever: no (house-edge band × max-bet cap) cell holds FUN ∧ SAFE ∧ SINK for ANY payout shape in the grid); the named non-odds levers ride to the World seat with the quantified gap: (i) rake-only PvP framing — priced FREE by the stated identity (even-money PvP with pot-rake r is G1 at e = r for each symmetric player: at r = 0.05 the measured row is FUN 0.2738 / P_double 0.0899 exact, and the house's rake take is risk-free, making SINK structural rather than statistical), (ii) session comp/stipend, (iii) entry-fee-with-prize shapes (both convert the SAFE failure from an unbounded bankroll event into a bounded fee — the one thing no in-grid cell could do); RIDER, measured: any surviving wager surface should pin MAXBET ≤ 0.05·B₀ for SAFE reasons alone (the tight cap tames capped-martingale wipe to 0.007 at the near-miss cell; at m ≥ 0.25 martingale wipes 0.18–0.98 of casual sessions); boundaries restated per the done-when: all numbers bankroll-RELATIVE — nothing here prices the casino sink against fishing/mining faucet mint in absolute chips/hr, the live earn-rate baseline whose absence V001 and V008 both named stays walled and their telemetry caveat applies verbatim; bets are i.i.d. with strategy-spread folded into the e-grid; the FUN line is the pre-registered disputable proxy with full curves shipped (no plausible re-draw rescues the envelope — SAFE and SINK carry the emptiness); question: Under the pinned ticket-frame model (B₀ = 1,000 integer chips; ticket price F = 0.01·B₀ = 10, a table constant no policy can escalate; prize schedules paying multiples of F with probabilities scaled by (1−t) so E[prize] = (1−t)·F exactly — T1 double-up {2F w.p. (1−t)/2, the even-money shape whose FUN leg is the IDENTICAL binomial to VERDICT 022's G1 reference, a pre-registered cross-verdict identity}, T2 tiered {8F, 3F, 1F w.p. (1−t)·{0.05, 0.10, 0.30}, per-ticket variance 3.4·F² at t=0}, T3 jackpot {25F, 5F w.p. (1−t)·{0.024, 0.08}, variance 16·F²}; take grid t ∈ {0.01, 0.02, 0.05, 0.10} + t=0 control reporting-only; house table rule per-round ticket cap c ∈ {5, 25, 100} — max per-round spend {5%, 25%, 100%}·B₀, the exact mirror of the parent's m-grid; re-buy policies with b ≤ c and b ≤ ⌊bankroll/F⌋, a round's b tickets resolving as b independent draws, round net = Σ prizes − b·F: R1 b=1, R5 b=min(5,·), RG greedy b=max affordable (the compounding all-in), MC chase b=min(2^L,·) with L = consecutive net-losing rounds reset on a net win (ticket-count martingale); profiles CASUAL 100 rounds or bankroll < F with P_ahead = P(final > B₀) and P_wipe = P(final ≤ 0.1·B₀), GRINDER to ≥ 2·B₀ or ≤ 0.5·B₀ hard-capped at 4,000 rounds with P_double and > 1% cap-hits marking the cell indeterminate (a NULL path, never silently absorbed;
